<s> ALFRED BURTON CHAPTER I THE FRUIT OF THE TREE Mr Alfred Burton, although he was blissfully and completely ignorant of the fact, stood at the door of Fate </s>
<s> He was a little out of breath and his silk hat was reclining at the back of his head </s>
<s> In his mouth was a large cigar which he felt certain was going to disagree with him, but he smoked it because it had been presented to him a few minutes ago by the client upon whom he was in attendance </s>
<s> He had rather deep-set blue eyes, which might have been attractive but for a certain keenness in their outlook, which was in a sense indicative of the methods and character of the young man himself; a pale, characterless face, a straggling, sandy moustache, and an earnest, not to say convincing, manner </s>
<s> He was dressed in such garments as the head-clerk of Messrs </s>
<s> Waddington & Forbes, third-rate auctioneers and house agents, might have been expected to select </s>
<s> He dangled a bunch of keys in his hand </s>
<s> "If this house don't suit you, sir," he declared, confidently, "why, there isn't one in the whole west-end that will </s>
<s> That's my opinion, anyway </s>
<s> There's nothing in our books to compare with it for value and accommodation </s>
<s> We nearly let it last week to Lord Leconside, but Her Ladyship--she came round with me herself--decided that it was just a trifle too large </s>
<s> As a matter of fact, sir," this energetic young man went on, confidentially, "the governor insisted upon a deposit and it didn't seem to be exactly convenient </s>
<s> It isn't always these people with titles who've got the money </s>
<s> That we find out in our business, sir, as quickly as anybody </s>
<s> As for the steam heating you were talking about, Mr Lynn, why, that's all very well for New York," he continued, persuasively, "but over here the climate doesn't call for it--you can take it from me that it doesn't, indeed, Mr Lynn </s>
<s> I have the letting in my hands of as many houses as most people, and you can take it from me, sir, as the direct result of my experience, that over here they won't have it--won't have it at any price, sir </s>
<s> Most unhealthy we find it, and always produces a rare crop of colds and coughs unknown to those that are used to an honest coal fire </s>
<s> It's all a matter of climate, sir, after all, isn't it" </s>
<s> The young man paused to take breath </s>
<s> His client, who had been listening attentively in gloomy but not unappreciative silence, removed his cigar from his mouth </s>
<s> He was a middle-aged American with a wife and daughters on their way over from New York, and his business was to take a house before they arrived </s>
<s> It wasn't a job he liked, but he was making the best of it </s>
<s> This young man appealed to his sense of business </s>
<s> "Say," he remarked, approvingly, "you've learned how to talk in your trade" </s>
<s> Stimulated by this encouragement, Alfred Burton clapped on his hat a little more securely, took a long breath, and went at it again </s>
<s> "Why, I'm giving myself a rest this morning, sir" </s>
<s> he declared </s>
<s> "I haven't troubled to tell you more than the bare facts </s>
<s> This house doesn't need any talking about--doesn't need a word said about it </s>
<s> Her Ladyship's last words to us were--Lady Idlemay, you know, the owner of the house--'Mr Waddington and Mr Burton,' she said--she was speaking to us both, for the governor always introduces me to clients as being the one who does most of the letting,--'Mr Waddington and Mr Burton,' she said, 'if a tenant comes along whom you think I'd like to have living in my rooms and using my furniture, breathing my air, so to speak, why, go ahead and let the house, rents being shockingly low just now, with agricultural depression and what not, but sooner than not let it to gentlepeople, I'll do without the money,' Her Ladyship declared </s>
<s> Now you're just the sort of tenant she'd like to have here </s>
<s> I'm quite sure of that, Mr Lynn </s>
<s> I should take a pleasure in bringing you two together" </s>
<s> Mr Lynn grunted </s>
<s> He was perfectly well aware that the house would seem more desirable to his wife and daughters from the very fact that it belonged to a "Lady" anybody </s>
<s> He was perfectly well aware, also, that his companion had suspected this </s>
<s> The consideration of these facts left him, however, unaffected </s>
<s> He was disposed, if anything, to admire the cleverness of the young man who had realized an outside asset </s>
<s> "Well, I've seen pretty well all over it," he remarked </s>
<s> "I'll go back to the office with you, anyhow, and have a word with Mr Waddington </s>
<s> By the way, what's that room behind you" </s>
<s> The young man glanced carelessly around at the door of the room of Fate and down at the bunch of keys which he held in his hand </s>
<s> He even chuckled as he replied </s>
<s> "I was going to mention the matter of that room, sir," he replied, "because, if perfectly agreeable to the tenant, Her Ladyship would like to keep it locked up" </s>
<s> "Locked up" </s>
<s> Mr Lynn repeated </s>
<s> "And why" </s>
<s> "Regular queer story, sir," the young man declared, confidentially </s>
<s> "The late Earl was a great traveller in the East, as you may have heard, and he was always poking about in some ruined city or other in the desert, and picking up things and making discoveries </s>
<s> Well, last time he came home from abroad, he brought with him an old Egyptian or Arab,--I don't know which he was, but he was brown,--settled him down in this room--in his own house, mind--and wouldn't have him disturbed or interfered with, not at any price </s>
<s> Well, the old chap worked here night and day at some sort of writing, and then, naturally enough, what with not having the sort of grub he liked, and never going outside the doors, he croaked" </s>
<s> "He what" </s>
<s> Mr Lynn interposed </s>
<s> "He died," the young man explained </s>
<s> "It was just about the time that the Earl was ill himself </s>
<s> His Lordship gave orders that the body was to be buried and the room locked up, in case the old chap's heirs should come along </s>
<s> Seems he'd brought a few odd things of his own over--nothing whatever of any value </s>
<s> Anyway, those were Lord Idlemay's wishes, and the room has been locked up ever since" </s>
<s> Mr Lynn was interested </s>
<s> "No objection to our just looking inside, I suppose" </s>
<s> "None whatever," the young man declared, promptly </s>
<s> "I was going to have a peep myself </s>
<s> Here goes" </s>
<s> He fitted the key in the lock and pushed the door open </s>
<s> Mr Lynn took one step forward and drew back hurriedly </s>
<s> "Thanks" </s>
<s> he said </s>
<s> "That'll do </s>
<s> I've seen all I want--and smelt" </s>
<s> Mr Alfred Burton, fortunately or unfortunately, was possessed of less sensitive nasal organs and an indomitable curiosity </s>
<s> The room was dark and stuffy, and a wave of pungent odor swept out upon them with the opening of the door </s>
<s> Nevertheless, he did not immediately close it </s>
<s> "One moment" </s>
<s> he muttered, peering inside </s>
<s> "I'll just look around and see that everything is in order" </s>
<s> He crossed the threshold and passed into the room </s>
<s> It was certainly a curious apartment </s>
<s> The walls were hung not with paper at all, but with rugs of some Oriental material which had the effect of still further increasing the gloom </s>
<s> There were neither chairs nor tables--no furniture at all, in fact, of any account but in the furthest corner was a great pile of cushions, and on the floor by the side a plain strip of sandalwood, covered with a purple cloth, on which were several square-shaped sheets of paper, a brass inkstand, and a bundle of quill pens </s>
<s> On the extreme corner of this strip of wood, which seemed to have been used as a writing desk by some one reclining upon the cushions, was the strangest article of all </s>
<s> Alfred Burton stared at it with wide-open eyes </s>
<s> It was a tiny plant growing out of a small-sized flower-pot, with real green leaves and a cluster of queer little brown fruit hanging down from among them </s>
<s> "Jiminy" </s>
<s> the clerk exclaimed </s>
<s> "I say, Mr Lynn, sir" </s>
<s> But Mr Lynn had gone off to pace the dining-room once more </s>
<s> Burton moved slowly forward and stooped down over the cushions </s>
<s> He took up the sheets of paper which lay upon the slab of sandalwood </s>
<s> They were covered with wholly indecipherable characters save for the last page only, and there, even as he stood with it in his fingers, he saw, underneath the concluding paragraph of those unintelligible hieroglyphics, a few words of faintly traced English, laboriously printed, probably a translation </s>
<s> He struck a match and read them slowly out to himself: "It is finished </s>
<s> The nineteenth generation has triumphed </s>

<s> Mr Alfred Burton removed his silk hat and reflectively scratched his head </s>
<s> "Queer sort of joker he must have been," he remarked to himself </s>
<s> "I wonder what he was getting at" </s>
<s> His eyes fell upon the little tree </s>
<s> He felt the earth in the pot it was quite dry </s>
<s> Yet the tree itself was fresh and green </s>
<s> "Here goes for a brown bean," he continued, and plucked one </s>

<s> "Don't suppose it will do me any harm," he muttered, doubtfully </s>
<s> There was naturally no reply </s>
<s> Mr Alfred Burton laughed uneasily to himself </s>
<s> The shadows of the room and its curious perfume were a trifle disconcerting </s>
<s> "Risk it, anyway," he concluded </s>
<s> "Here goes" </s>
<s> He raised the little brown fruit--which did indeed somewhat resemble a bean--to his mouth and swallowed it </s>
<s> He found it quite tasteless, but the deed was no sooner done than he was startled by a curious buzzing in his ears and a momentary but peculiar lapse of memory </s>
<s> He sat and looked around him like a man who has been asleep and suddenly awakened in unfamiliar surroundings </s>
<s> Then the sound of his client's voice suddenly recalled him to himself </s>
<s> He started up and peered through the gloom </s>
<s> "Who's there" </s>
<s> he asked, sharply </s>
<s> "Say, young man, I am waiting for you when you're quite ready," Mr Lynn remarked from the threshold </s>

<s> Mr Alfred Burton came slowly out and locked the door of the room </s>

<s> Mr Alfred Burton shook his head doubtfully </s>
<s> "I don't think I would take it, if I were you, Mr Lynn," he said </s>
<s> Mr Lynn stopped short upon the pavement and looked at his companion in amazement </s>
<s> The latter had the air of one very little interested in the subject of conversation </s>
<s> He was watching approvingly a barrowful of lilac and other spring flowers being wheeled along by a flower-seller in the middle of the road </s>
<s> "What an exquisite perfume" </s>
<s> the young man murmured, enthusiastically </s>
<s> "Doesn't it remind you, Mr Lynn, of a beautiful garden somewhere right away in the country--one of those old-fashioned gardens, you know, with narrow paths where you have to push your way through the flowers, and where there are always great beds of pink and white stocks near the box edges </s>
<s> And do you notice--an accident, of course--but what a delicate blend of color the lilac and those yellow jonquils make" </s>

<s> "In one moment," Burton replied </s>

<s> He hastened across the street and returned a moment or two later with a bunch of violets in his hand </s>
<s> Mr Lynn watched him, partly in amazement, partly in disapproval </s>
<s> There seemed to be very little left of the smart, businesslike young man whose methods, only a short time ago, had commanded his unwilling admiration </s>
<s> Mr Alfred Burton's expression had undergone a complete change </s>

<s> A pleasant but somewhat abstracted smile had taken the place of his forced amiability </s>

<s> You see, it is not generally known, but there is no doubt that Lord Idlemay had typhoid fever there" </s>
<s> "Typhoid" </s>
<s> Mr Lynn exclaimed, incredulously </s>
<s> His companion nodded </s>
<s> "Two of the servants were down with it as well," he continued </s>
<s> "We implored Lady Idlemay, when she offered us the letting of the house, to have the drains put in thorough order, but when we got the estimate out for her she absolutely declined </s>
<s> To tell you the truth, the best agents had all refused, under the circumstances, to have the house upon their books at all </s>

<s> Mr Lynn removed the cigar from his mouth for a moment </s>
<s> There was a slight frown Upon his forehead </s>
<s> He was puzzled </s>
<s> "Say, you're not getting at me for any reason, are you" </s>
<s> he demanded </s>
<s> "My dear sir" </s>

<s> "I am simply doing my duty and telling you the truth </s>
<s> The house is not in a fit state to be let to any one--certainly not to a man with a family </s>

<s> CHAPTER II A TRANSFORMATION Burton stood for a moment upon the threshold of the office, looking around him </s>
<s> A new and peculiar distaste for these familiar surroundings seemed suddenly to have sprung into life </s>
<s> For the first time he realized the intense ugliness of this scene of his daily labors </s>
<s> The long desk, ink-splashed and decrepit, was covered with untidy piles of papers, some of them thick with dust; the walls were hung with seedy-looking files and an array of tattered bills; there were cobwebs in every corner, gaps in the linoleum floor-covering </s>
<s> In front of the office-boy--a youth about fourteen years of age, who represented the remaining clerical staff of the establishment--were pinned up several illustrations cut out from _Comic Cuts_, the _Police News_, and various other publications of a similar order </s>
<s> As Burton looked around him, his distaste grew </s>
<s> It seemed impossible that he had ever existed for an hour amid such an environment </s>
<s> The prospect of the future was suddenly hugely distasteful </s>
<s> Very slowly he changed his coat and climbed on to his worn horsehair stool, without exchanging his usual facetious badinage with the remaining member of the staff </s>
<s> The office-boy, who had thought of something good to say, rather resented his silence </s>
<s> It forced him into taking the initiative, a position which placed him from the first at a disadvantage </s>
<s> "Any luck with the Yank, Mr Burton" </s>
<s> he inquired, with anxious civility </s>
<s> Burton shook his head </s>
<s> "None at all," he confessed </s>
<s> "He wouldn't have anything to do with the house" </s>
<s> "Has any one been letting on to him about it, do you think" </s>
<s> "I don't think so," Burton replied </s>
<s> "I don't think any one else has mentioned it to him at all </s>
<s> He seems to be a complete stranger here" </s>
<s> "Couldn't have been quite at your best, could you, Mr Burton, sir </s>
<s> Not your usual bright and eloquent self, eh" </s>
<s> The boy grinned and then ducked, expecting a missile </s>
<s> None came, however </s>
<s> Alfred Burton was in a very puzzled state of mind, and he neither showed nor indeed felt any resentment </s>
<s> He turned and faced his subordinate </s>
<s> "I really don't know, Clarkson," he admitted </s>
<s> "I am sure that I was quite polite, and I showed him everything he wished to see; but, of course, I had to tell him the truth about the place" </s>
<s> "The what" </s>
<s> young Clarkson inquired, in a mystified tone </s>
<s> "The truth," Burton repeated </s>
<s> "Wot yer mean" </s>
<s> "About the typhoid and that," Burton explained, mildly </s>
<s> The office-boy pondered for a moment </s>
<s> Then he slowly opened a ledger, drew a day-book towards him, and continued his work </s>
<s> He was being jollied, of course, but the thing was too subtle for him at present </s>
<s> He decided to wait for the next move </s>
<s> Burton continued to regard his subordinate, however, and by degrees an expression of pained disapproval crept into his face </s>
<s> "Clarkson," he said, "if you will forgive my mentioning a purely personal matter, why do you wear such uncomfortable collars and such an exceedingly unbecoming tie" </s>
<s> The office-boy swung round upon his stool </s>
<s> His mouth was wide open like a rabbit's </s>
<s> He fingered the offending articles </s>
<s> "What's the matter with them" </s>
<s> he demanded, getting his question out with a single breath </s>
<s> "Your collars are much too high," Burton pointed out </s>
<s> "One can see how they cut into your neck </s>
<s> Then why wear a tie of that particular shade of vivid purple when your clothes themselves, with that blue and yellow stripe, are somewhat noticeable </s>
<s> There is a lack of symphony about the arrangement, an entire absence of taste, which is apt to depress one </s>
<s> The whole effect which you produce upon one's vision is abominable </s>
<s> You won't think my mentioning this a liberty, I hope" </s>
<s> "What about your own red tie and dirty collar" </s>
<s> young Clarkson asked, indignantly </s>
<s> "What price your eight and sixpenny trousers, eh, with the blue stripe and the grease stains </s>
<s> What about the sham diamond stud in your dickey, and your three inches of pinned on cuff </s>
<s> Fancy your appearance, perhaps </s>
<s> Why, I wouldn't walk the streets in such a rig-out" </s>
<s> Burton listened to his junior's attack unresentingly but with increasing bewilderment </s>
<s> Then he slipped from his seat and walked hurriedly across to the looking-glass, which he took down from its nail </s>

<s> He was plain, of insignificant appearance, he was ill and tastelessly dressed </s>
<s> He stood there before the sixpenny-ha'penny mirror and drank the cup of humiliation </s>
<s> "Calling my tie, indeed" </s>
<s> the office-boy muttered, his smouldering resentment bringing him back to the attack </s>
<s> "Present from my best girl, that was, and she knows what's what </s>
<s> Young lady with a place in a west-end milliner's shop, too </s>
<s> If that doesn't mean good taste, I should like to know what does </s>
<s> Look at your socks, too, all coming down over the tops of your boots </s>

<s> "I am sorry I spoke, Clarkson," he apologized humbly </s>
<s> "It certainly seemed to have slipped my memory that I myself--I can't think how I managed to make such hideous, unforgivable mistakes" </s>

<s> Burton made no reply </s>
<s> He was down and his junior kicked him </s>

<s> "Why don't you chuck that rotten dickey away </s>
<s> Cave" </s>
<s> The door leading into the private office was brusquely opened </s>
<s> Mr Waddington, the only existing member of the firm, entered---a large, untidy-looking man, also dressed in most uncomely fashion, and wearing an ill-brushed silk hat on the back of his head </s>

<s> "Well, did you land him" </s>

<s> "It was quite impossible to interest him in the house at all, sir," he declared </s>

<s> Mr Waddington's face fell </s>

<s> CHAPTER V BURTON'S NEW LIFE Burton spent the rest of the day in most delightful fashion </s>
<s> He took the Tube to South Kensington Museum, where he devoted himself for several hours to the ecstatic appreciation of a small section of its treasures </s>
<s> He lunched off some fruit and tea and bread and butter out in the gardens, wandering about afterwards among the flower-beds and paying especial and delighted attention to the lilac trees beyond the Memorial </s>
<s> Towards evening he grew depressed </s>
<s> The memory of Ellen, of little Alfred, and his gingerbread villa, became almost like a nightmare to him </s>
<s> And then the light came </s>
<s> His great resolution was formed </s>
<s> With beating heart he turned to a stationer's shop, bought a sheet of paper and an envelope, borrowed a pen and wrote: My DEAR ELLEN, I am not coming home for a short time </s>
<s> As you remarked, there is something the matter with me </s>
<s> I don't know what it is </s>
<s> Perhaps in a few days I shall find out </s>
<s> I shall send your money as usual on Saturday, and hope that you and the boy will continue well </s>
<s> From your husband, ALFRED BURTON </s>
<s> Burton sighed a long sigh of intense relief as he folded up and addressed this epistle </s>
<s> Then he bought four stamps and sent it home </s>
<s> He was a free man </s>
<s> He had three pounds fifteen in his pocket, a trifle of money in the savings-bank, no situation, and a wife and son to support </s>
<s> The position was serious enough, yet never for a moment could he regard it without a new elasticity of spirit and a certain reckless optimism, the source of which he did not in the least understand </s>
<s> He was to learn before long, however, that moods and their resulting effect upon the spirit were part of the penalty which he must pay for the greater variety of his new life </s>
<s> He took a tiny bedroom somewhere Westminster way--a room in a large, solemn-looking house, decayed and shabby, but still showing traces of its former splendor </s>
<s> That night he saw an Ibsen play from the front row of a deserted gallery, and afterwards, in melancholy mood, he walked homeward along the Embankment by the moonlight </s>
<s> For the first time in life he had come face to face with a condition of which he had had no previous experience--the condition of intellectual pessimism </s>
<s> He was depressed because in this new and more spontaneous world, so full of undreamed-of beauties, so exquisitely stimulating to his new powers of appreciation, he had found something which he did not understand </s>
<s> Truth for the first time had seemed unpleasant, not only in its effects but in itself </s>
<s> The problem was beyond him </s>

<s> CHAPTER VI A MEETING WITH ELLEN The clearness of vision which enabled Alfred Burton now to live in and appreciate a new and marvelous world, failed, however, to keep him from feeling, occasionally, exceedingly hungry </s>
<s> He lived on very little, but the weekly amount must always be sent to Garden Green </s>

<s> CHAPTER XIX A BAD HALF-HOUR Burton slept that night under a gorse bush </s>
<s> He was no sooner alone on the great unlit Common with its vast sense of spaciousness, its cool silence, its splendid dome of starlit sky, than all his anger and disappointment seemed to pass away </s>
<s> The white, threatening faces of the professor and Mr Bomford no longer haunted him </s>

<s> Even the gorse bushes creaked and quivered </s>

<s> Then he rose to his feet, took in a long breath of the fresh morning air, and started briskly across the Common towards the nearest railway station </s>
<s> He was conscious, after the first few steps, of a dim premonition of some coming change </s>
<s> It did not affect--indeed, it seemed to increase the lightness of his spirits, yet he was conscious at the back of his brain of a fear which he could not put into words </s>
<s> The first indication of real trouble came in the fact that he found himself whistling "Yip-i-addy-i-ay" as he turned into the station yard </s>
<s> He knew then what was coming </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXI AN AMAZING TRANSFORMATION The novel which was to bring immortal fame and, incidentally, freedom from all financial responsibilities, to Burton, came back within a week, with a polite note which he was at first inclined to accept as some consolation until he found that it was stereotyped </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXIII CONDEMNED </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXIV MENATOGEN, THE MIND FOOD It had been a dinner of celebration </s>
